[mol_theme] {
  --gd_kit_theme_success: hsl( calc( var(--mol_theme_hue) + 250deg ), 90%, calc( 60% - 20% * var(--mol_theme_luma)) );
  --gd_kit_theme_error: hsl( calc( var(--mol_theme_hue) + 140deg ), 90%, calc( 60% - 20% * var(--mol_theme_luma)) );
  --gd_kit_theme_warn: hsl( calc( var(--mol_theme_hue) + 200deg ), 90%, calc( 60% - 20% * var(--mol_theme_luma)) );
}

      'error',
      'success',

  export class $gd_avatar_pane extends $.$gd_avatar_pane {
    @ $mol_mem
    init() {
      return this.$.$gd_avatar.make({
        dom_node: () => this.dom_node(),
      })
    }

    model() {
      return this.init().instance()
    }

    @ $mol_mem
    resize_sync() {
      const rec = this.view_rect()
      if (rec) this.model().onResize(rec.width, rec.height)
    }

    auto() {
      this.resize_sync()
    }

    override render() {
      this.model()

      return super.render()
    }
  }

$gd_avatar_bubble $mol_view
  minimal_width 700
  minimal_height 600
  pressed? false
  event *
    mouseup? <=> mouseup? null
    mousedown? <=> mousedown? null
    mousemove? <=> mousemove? null
  sub /
    <= Avatar $mol_view
      theme \$mol_theme_card
      minimal_width 40
      minimal_height 80
      style *
        top <= top? 0
        left <= left? 0


  
export class $gd_avatar_bubble extends $.$gd_avatar_bubble {
    override mousedown( e: Event ) {
      this.pressed(true)
    }

    override mouseup( e: Event ) {
      this.pressed(false)
    }

    override mousemove( e: MouseEvent ) {
      if (! this.pressed()) return
      this.left(e.clientX + 'px')
      this.top(e.clientY + 'px')
    }

  }


  $mol_style_define( $gd_avatar_bubble, {
    Avatar: {
      position: 'absolute',
      zIndex: 100,
    },
  } )
